Copy
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'react-native-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function SeekerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'seeker' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [bio, setBio] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, bio, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBio(data.bio || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibrary({
      mediaType: 'photo',
      quality: 0.8,
      includeBase64: false,
    });
    console.log('ImagePicker result:', result); // Debug result
    if (!result.didCancel && result.assets) {
      setProfilePic(result.assets[0].uri);
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        const file = {
          uri: result.assets[0].uri,
          name: `profile-${user.id}.jpg`,
          type: 'image/jpeg',
        };
        const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .upload(`public/${file.name}`, file);
        if (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Upload failed: ' + uploadError.message);
        } else {
          const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .getPublicUrl(`public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: urlData.publicUrl })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
          } else {
            Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
          }
        }
      }
    } else if (result.didCancel) {
      console.log('Image pick cancelled');
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image, check permissions.');
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, bio })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Success', 'Logged out!');
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={bio}
            onChangeText={setBio}
            placeholder="Bio (Short background)"
            multiline
          />
          {bio.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles
const localStyles = StyleSheet.create({
  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',
    marginBottom: 20,
  },
  scrollContainer: {
    padding: 20,
  },
  bioContainer: {
    position: 'relative',
    marginBottom: 10,
  },
  checkmark: {
    position: 'absolute',
    right: 10,
    top: '50%',
    transform: [{ translateY: -15 }],
    backgroundColor: '#48d22b',
    borderRadius: 15,
    width: 30,
    height: 30,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  checkmarkText: {
    color: '#fff',
    fontSize: 20,
  },
});

Thanks for the update and for sharing the logs! It’s great that the gallery is opening now, but the setSelectedImage error suggests the code is trying to use a non-existent state variable (likely from your neighbor’s changes). The expo-image-picker warning about MediaTypeOptions is also easy to fix. Let’s update SeekerProfileScreen.js to use the correct state (profilePic) and fix the deprecated media type.

Step 1: Update SeekerProfileScreen.js to fix the image picker logic. Replace its content with this:

javascript

Collapse

Unwrap

Run

Copy
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function SeekerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'seeker' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [bio, setBio] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, bio, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBio(data.bio || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images, // Use deprecated option for now
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        setProfilePic(result.assets[0].uri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const file = {
            uri: result.assets[0].uri,
            name: `profile-${user.id}.jpg`,
            type: 'image/jpeg',
          };
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(`public/${file.name}`, file);
          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Upload failed: ' + uploadError.message);
          } else {
            const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .getPublicUrl(`public/${file.name}`);
            const { error: updateError } = await supabase
              .from('users')
              .update({ profile_pics: urlData.publicUrl })
              .eq('id', user.id);
            if (updateError) {
              console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
            } else {
              Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
            }
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, bio })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Success', 'Logged out!');
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={bio}
            onChangeText={setBio}
            placeholder="Bio (Short background)"
            multiline
          />
          {bio.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles
const localStyles = StyleSheet.create({
  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',
    marginBottom: 20,
  },
  scrollContainer: {
    padding: 20,
  },
  bioContainer: {
    position: 'relative',
    marginBottom: 10,
  },
  checkmark: {
    position: 'absolute',
    right: 10,
    top: '50%',
    transform: [{ translateY: -15 }],
    backgroundColor: '#48d22b',
    borderRadius: 15,
    width: 30,
    height: 30,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  checkmarkText: {
    color: '#fff',
    fontSize: 20,
  },
});

Alright! The image now loads on the phone!

Seems we have a supabase issue now:
 LOG  Upload error: new row violates row-level security policy




Awesome, glad the image picker is working! The new row violates row-level security policy error means the Supabase storage bucket (pics) has a Row-Level Security (RLS) policy that’s blocking the upload. Let’s fix this by updating the storage policy to allow authenticated users to upload to the public folder in the pics bucket.

Step 1: Update the storage policy in Supabase. Go to your Supabase dashboard, navigate to Storage > Policies > pics bucket, and add this policy:

Policy Name: Allow authenticated uploads
Allowed Operation: INSERT
Expression:
sql



auth.role() = 'authenticated'
Target Roles: authenticated
Next Action: Add this policy in the Supabase dashboard, then test the image upload again on Expo Go via USB. Let me know the outcome (e.g., upload works, or any new errors/logs). If you’re unsure how to set the policy, I can provide detailed steps!








5.7s
Can you perhaps provide the sql for the policiy?




Sure thing! Here’s the SQL to create a policy for the pics bucket in Supabase to allow authenticated users to upload files to the public folder.

Step 1: Run this SQL command in the Supabase SQL Editor:

sql

Collapse

Unwrap

Copy
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated uploads" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT
TO authenticated
WITH CHECK (
  bucket_id = 'pics'
  AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public'
);
Next Action: Execute this in the Supabase SQL Editor, then test the image upload again on Expo Go via USB. Let me know the outcome (e.g., upload works, or any new errors/logs).

import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });

              .from('users')

              console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
            } else {
              Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
            }
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Success', 'Logged out!');

    Keyboard.dismiss();

Step 1: Update EmployerProfileScreen.js to use business_name and fix the logout navigation. Replace its content with this:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        setProfilePic(result.assets[0].uri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const file = {
            uri: result.assets[0].uri,
            name: `profile-${user.id}.jpg`,
            type: 'image/jpeg',
          };
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(`public/${file.name}`, file);
          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Upload failed: ' + uploadError.message);
          } else {
            const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .getPublicUrl(`public/${file.name}`);
            const { error: updateError } = await supabase
              .from('users')
              .update({ profile_pics: urlData.publicUrl })
              .eq('id', user.id);
            if (updateError) {
              console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
            } else {
              Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
            }
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Success', 'Logged out!');
      navigation.replace('Welcome');
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles
const localStyles = StyleSheet.create({
  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',
    marginBottom: 20,
  },
  scrollContainer: {
    padding: 20,
  },
  bioContainer: {
    position: 'relative',
    marginBottom: 10,
  },
  checkmark: {
    position: 'absolute',
    right: 10,

Replace EmployerProfileScreen.js with this:

javascript

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched profile_pics:', data.profile_pics); // Debug log
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        setProfilePic(result.assets[0].uri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const file = {
            uri: result.assets[0].uri,
            name: `profile-${user.id}.jpg`,
            type: 'image/jpeg',
          };
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(`public/${file.name}`, file, { upsert: true }); // Allow overwrite
          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Upload failed: ' + uploadError.message);
          } else {
            const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .getPublicUrl(`public/${file.name}`);
            const { error: updateError } = await supabase
              .from('users')
              .update({ profile_pics: urlData.publicUrl })
              .eq('id', user.id);
            if (updateError) {
              console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
            } else {
              Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
            }
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles
const localStyles = StyleSheet.create({
  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',
    marginBottom: 20,
  },
  scrollContainer: {
    padding: 20,
  },
  bioContainer: {
    position: 'relative',
    marginBottom: 10,
  },
  checkmark: {
    position: 'absolute',
    right: 10,
    top: '50%',
    transform: [{ translateY: -15 }],
    backgroundColor: '#48d22b',
    borderRadius: 15,
    width: 30,
    height: 30,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  checkmarkText: {
    color: '#fff',
    fontSize: 20,
  },
});

Also, check the console logs for Fetched profile_pics to see what’s being pulled from Supabase. import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched data:', data); // Debug full data
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          setProfilePic(data.profile_pics || null);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        setProfilePic(result.assets[0].uri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const file = {
            uri: result.assets[0].uri,
            name: `profile-${user.id}.jpg`,
            type: 'image/jpeg',
          };
          // Try removing existing file first
          await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove([`public/${file.name}`]);
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(`public/${file.name}`, file, { upsert: true });
          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Upload failed: ' + uploadError.message);
          } else {
            const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .getPublicUrl(`public/${file.name}`);
            console.log('Public URL:', urlData.publicUrl); // Debug URL
            const { error: updateError } = await supabase
              .from('users')
              .update({ profile_pics: urlData.publicUrl })
              .eq('id', user.id);
            if (updateError) {
              console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
            } else {
              Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
            }
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles

  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',

Thanks for the update and the logs! The issues persist: the profile pic is blank (flashing then disappearing), the upload fails with "The resource already exists," and the bio field is still showing instead of business_name. Additionally, you mentioned needing viewers to access images, which requires a SELECT policy for the storage bucket, and you recall having three policies in the previous project. Let’s address these step-by-step, starting with the storage policies to fix the upload and viewing issues, then tackle the profile pic and field display.

Analysis
Upload error: "The resource already exists": The upsert: true option should allow overwriting, but it’s not working, likely due to a missing UPDATE policy for the pics bucket. Supabase requires SELECT and UPDATE permissions for upsert to work.supabase.com
Blank profile pic: The Fetched data log is missing, so we can’t see what profile_pics is returning. The flash-then-disappear suggests profile_pics might be an invalid URL or null.
Bio field showing: The EmployerProfileScreen.js code already uses business_name correctly, so the issue might be in AppNavigator.js or Supabase data fetching mixing up seeker and employer fields.
Storage policies: You mentioned three policies in the previous project. Typically, for a public bucket like pics, you need:
INSERT for uploading files.
SELECT for viewing files.
UPDATE for overwriting files (needed for upsert).supabase.com
Let’s add the missing policies and debug the profile pic issue.

Step 1: Add SELECT and UPDATE policies for the pics bucket in Supabase to allow viewing and overwriting files. Run these SQL commands in the Supabase SQL Editor:

sql

Collapse

Unwrap

Copy
-- Allow authenticated users to view files in the pics bucket
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated view" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT
TO authenticated
USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public');

-- Allow authenticated users to update (overwrite) files in the pics bucket
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated updates" ON storage.objects
FOR UPDATE
TO authenticated
USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public');

"mimeType": "image/jpeg", "rotation": null, "type": "image", "uri": "file:///data/user/0/host.exp.exponent/cache/ExperienceData/%2540anonymous%252Fizzijobs-2af31e08-7248-44d8-b132-1c529e4ee767/ImagePicker/2f23c1e9-21cc-4761-ade7-08c58dc86af5.jpeg", "width": 1280}], "canceled": false} 
 LOG  Upload error: The resource already exists




Great question! Yes, in the context of Supabase and database/storage operations, UPDATE is essentially the same as "edit." It refers to modifying an existing resource (like overwriting a file in storage or updating a row in a table). In our case, the UPDATE policy allows overwriting existing files in the pics bucket, which should fix the "The resource already exists" error.

The logs show the same issues as before: the profile pic is blank, the upload fails with "The resource already exists," and the bio field is still appearing (you confirmed it’s still showing instead of Business Name). The Invalid login credentials log suggests a brief login hiccup, but since you logged in successfully as an employer, we’ll focus on the profile issues.

Analysis
Upload error: The UPDATE policy was added, but the error persists. This could be because the remove step before uploading isn’t working due to a missing DELETE policy, or the upsert option isn’t being applied correctly.
Blank profile pic: The Fetched data log is still missing, so we don’t know what profile_pics is returning. The flash-then-disappear suggests the URL might be invalid or not saved correctly.
Bio field: The EmployerProfileScreen.js code uses business_name, but if bio is showing, the role logic in AppNavigator.js might be incorrect, loading the SeekerProfileScreen instead.
Logout navigation: Still not navigating to the Welcome screen, likely due to navigation context or timing.
Let’s add a DELETE policy to ensure the remove step works, and update AppNavigator.js to debug the role logic.

Step 1: Add a DELETE policy for the pics bucket in Supabase to allow removing existing files. Run this SQL command in the Supabase SQL Editor:

sql

Collapse

Unwrap

Copy
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated deletes" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE
TO authenticated
USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public');

Below is the EmployerProfile screen from the previous project. Does this givve you any clues in fixing our issue?

import * as React from 'react';
import { View, Text, ScrollView, Image, Alert, Platform, TouchableOpacity } from 'react-native';
import { TextInput, Button } from 'react-native-paper';
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import { supabase } from '../utils/supabaseClient';
import { Alert as RNAlert } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import { styles } from '../theme/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen({ route }) {
  const { userId } = route.params || {};
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState({ name: '', phone: '', location: '', profile_pic: null, business_name: '' });
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState({});

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchProfile = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      const effectiveUserId = userId || '73b5b857-2107-41f4-bce4-f6961fa2d285';
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .select('name, mobile_number, location, profile_pic, business_name')
        .eq('id', effectiveUserId)
        .single();
      if (error) console.log('Error fetching profile:', error.message);
      else {
        console.log('Fetched profile data:', data);
        setProfile({
          name: data?.name || '',
          phone: data?.mobile_number || '',
          location: data?.location || '',
          profile_pic: data?.profile_pic ? data.profile_pic : null,
          business_name: data?.business_name || '',
        });
        if (data.profile_pic) {
          const fileName = data.profile_pic.split('/').pop();
          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('profiles')
            .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pic, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL Error:', urlError.message);
            setProfile((prev) => ({ ...prev, profile_pic: null }));
          } else {
            setProfile((prev) => ({ ...prev, profile_pic: urlData.signedUrl }));
          }
        }
      }
      setLoading(false);
    };
    fetchProfile();
    if (Platform.OS !== 'web') {
      ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync().then(({ status }) => {
        if (status !== 'granted') Alert.alert('Permission Required', 'Please allow access to your photos.');
      });
    }
  }, [userId]);

  const pickImage = async () => {
    let result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({ mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images, allowsEditing: true, aspect: [1, 1], quality: 0.5 });
    if (!result.canceled) {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const file = result.assets[0];
        const fileUri = file.uri;
        console.log('Selected image URI:', fileUri);
        const fileInfo = await FileSystem.getInfoAsync(fileUri);
        console.log('Original file size:', fileInfo.size, 'bytes');
        const { data: { session }, error: sessionError } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
        if (sessionError || !session) throw new Error('No active session');
        const effectiveUserId = userId || '73b5b857-2107-41f4-bce4-f6961fa2d285';
        const fileName = `${effectiveUserId}/profile-pic-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        const fileExt = fileUri.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
        const mimeType = fileExt === 'jpg' || fileExt === 'jpeg' ? 'image/jpeg' : fileExt === 'png' ? 'image/png' : 'image/jpeg';
        console.log('Uploading to Supabase with MIME type:', mimeType);

        const uploadResponse = await FileSystem.uploadAsync(
          `https://hceoednqxvubealrjhkf.supabase.co/storage/v1/object/profiles/${fileName}`,
          fileUri,
          { headers: { 'Content-Type': mimeType, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${session.access_token}` }, httpMethod: 'PUT', uploadType: FileSystem.FileSystemUploadType.BINARY_CONTENT }
        );
        if (uploadResponse.status !== 200) throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${uploadResponse.body}`);
        console.log('Upload successful, response:', uploadResponse.body);
        const { data: urlData, error: signedUrlError } = await supabase.storage.from('profiles').createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
        if (signedUrlError) throw new Error('Failed to generate signed URL');
        console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);
        await supabase.from('users').update({ profile_pic: fileName }).eq('id', effectiveUserId);
        setProfile((prev) => ({ ...prev, profile_pic: urlData.signedUrl }));
        RNAlert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
      } catch (error) {
        console.log('Image Pick Error:', error.message);
        RNAlert.alert('Error', `Network request failed: ${error.message}`);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
  };

  const validate = () => {
    const newErrors = {};
    if (!profile.name.trim()) newErrors.name = 'Name is required';
    if (!profile.phone.trim()) newErrors.phone = 'Phone number is required';
    else if (!/^\+?[1-9]\d{9,14}$/.test(profile.phone)) newErrors.phone = 'Invalid phone number';
    if (!profile.location.trim()) newErrors.location = 'Targeted Job Location is required';
    return newErrors;
  };

  const saveProfile = async () => {
    const newErrors = validate();
    if (Object.keys(newErrors).length > 0) {
      setErrors(newErrors);
      return;
    }
    console.log('Saving profile with:', { name: profile.name, phone: profile.phone, location: profile.location, business_name: profile.business_name });
    try {
      const effectiveUserId = userId || '73b5b857-2107-41f4-bce4-f6961fa2d285';
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name: profile.name, mobile_number: profile.phone, location: profile.location, business_name: profile.business_name })
        .eq('id', effectiveUserId)
        .select();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Supabase update error:', error.message, error.code, error.details);
        throw error;
      }
      console.log('Profile updated successfully:', data);
      RNAlert.alert('Success', 'Profile updated!');
    } catch (error) {
      RNAlert.alert('Error', error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) throw error;
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    } catch (error) {
      RNAlert.alert('Error', error.message);
    }
  };

  if (loading) return <Text>Loading...</Text>;

  return (
    <ScrollView style={styles.container} contentContainerStyle={[styles.scrollContent, { justifyContent: 'center' }]}>
      {/* Removed <Text style={styles.title}>Employer Profile</Text> */}
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={pickImage} style={[styles.profilePicContainer, { marginTop: 20 }]}>
  <Image
    source={profile.profile_pic ? { uri: profile.profile_pic } : require('../../assets/default-avatar.png')}
    style={styles.profilePic}
    onError={(e) => {
      console.log('Image Load Error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
      setProfile((prev) => ({ ...prev, profile_pic: require('../../assets/default-avatar.png') }));
    }}
  />
</TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput
        label="Name"
        value={profile.name}
        onChangeText={(text) => { setProfile({ ...profile, name: text }); if (errors.name) setErrors({ ...errors, name: '' }); }}
        style={styles.input}
        error={!!errors.name}
      />
      {errors.name ? <Text style={styles.errorText}>{errors.name}</Text> : null}
      <TextInput
        label="Phone Number"
        value={profile.phone}
        onChangeText={(text) => { setProfile({ ...profile, phone: text }); if (errors.phone) setErrors({ ...errors, phone: '' }); }}
        style={styles.input}
        keyboardType="phone-pad"
        error={!!errors.phone}
      />
      {errors.phone ? <Text style={styles.errorText}>{errors.phone}</Text> : null}
      <TextInput
        label="Targeted Job Location"
        value={profile.location}
        onChangeText={(text) => { setProfile({ ...profile, location: text }); if (errors.location) setErrors({ ...errors, location: '' }); }}
        style={styles.input}
        error={!!errors.location}
      />
      {errors.location ? <Text style={styles.errorText}>{errors.location}</Text> : null}
      <TextInput
        label="Business Name (optional)"
        value={profile.business_name}
        onChangeText={(text) => setProfile({ ...profile, business_name: text })}
        style={styles.input}
      />
      <Button mode="contained" style={styles.saveButton} onPress={saveProfile} accessibilityLabel="Save profile">
        Save
      </Button>
      <Button mode="outlined" style={styles.logoutButton} onPress={handleLogout} accessibilityLabel="Logout">
        Logout
      </Button>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}




Thanks for sharing the previous project’s EmployerProfileScreen.js! It provides some great insights. The key differences in the previous project that likely made it work are:

Image upload: It uses FileSystem.uploadAsync with a direct HTTP request and a unique file name (profile-pic-${Date.now()}.jpg) to avoid conflicts, unlike our current supabase.storage.upload with a fixed name.
Profile pic handling: It uses signed URLs (createSignedUrl) for secure access, and the onError handler in the Image component falls back to the default avatar if the URL fails.
Storage bucket: It uses a profiles bucket instead of pics, but the logic is similar.
Navigation: The handleLogout uses navigation.reset correctly, which should work for navigation.
Fields: It correctly handles business_name and includes a location field, which we don’t have in the current project.
The current issues are:

Blank profile pic: Likely due to an invalid profile_pics URL or null value. The previous project’s onError handler and signed URLs could help.
Upload error ("The resource already exists"): The fixed file name (profile-${user.id}.jpg) causes conflicts. Using a unique name like the previous project should fix this.
Bio field showing: This suggests AppNavigator.js might be loading SeekerProfileScreen instead of EmployerProfileScreen. We’ll check the role logic.
Logout navigation: Should work with navigation.reset, but we’ll ensure it’s consistent.
Let’s update EmployerProfileScreen.js to adopt the previous project’s approach for image uploads and add error handling for the profile pic. We’ll also address the bio issue by checking AppNavigator.js next.

Step 1: Update EmployerProfileScreen.js to use unique file names, signed URLs, and add an onError handler. Replace its content with this:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              setProfilePic(null);
            } else {
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
          const fileExt = fileUri.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
          const mimeType = fileExt === 'jpg' || fileExt === 'jpeg' ? 'image/jpeg' : 'image/png';
          const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
          if (!session) throw new Error('No active session');
          const uploadResponse = await FileSystem.uploadAsync(
            `${supabase.storageUrl}/object/pics/${fileName}`,
            fileUri,
            {
              headers: {
                'Content-Type': mimeType,
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${session.access_token}`,
              },
              httpMethod: 'PUT',
              uploadType: FileSystem.FileSystemUploadType.BINARY_CONTENT,
            }
          );
          if (uploadResponse.status !== 200) throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${uploadResponse.body}`);
          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) throw new Error('Failed to generate signed URL');
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);
          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
          } else {
            setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
            onError={(e) => {
              console.log('Image Load Error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
              setProfilePic(null);
            }}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

// Local styles
const localStyles = StyleSheet.create({
  profilePic: {
    alignSelf: 'center',
    marginBottom: 20,
  },
  scrollContainer: {
    padding: 20,
  },
  bioContainer: {
    position: 'relative',
    marginBottom: 10,
  },
  checkmark: {
    position: 'absolute',
    right: 10,
    top: '50%',
    transform: [{ translateY: -15 }],
    backgroundColor: '#48d22b',
    borderRadius: 15,
    width: 30,
    height: 30,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  checkmarkText: {
    color: '#fff',
    fontSize: 20,
  },
});

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded with role:', role); // Debug role
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              setProfilePic(null);
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: [ImagePicker.MediaType.IMAGE], // Updated to fix warning
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
          const fileExt = fileUri.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
          const mimeType = fileExt === 'jpg' || fileExt === 'jpeg' ? 'image/jpeg' : 'image/png';
          const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
          if (!session) throw new Error('No active session');
          console.log('Attempting to remove file:', fileName);
          await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove([fileName]);
          const uploadResponse = await FileSystem.uploadAsync(
            `${supabase.storageUrl}/object/pics/${fileName}`,
            fileUri,
            {
              headers: {
                'Content-Type': mimeType,
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${session.access_token}`,
              },
              httpMethod: 'PUT',
              uploadType: FileSystem.FileSystemUploadType.BINARY_CONTENT,
            }
          );
          console.log('Upload response:', uploadResponse);
          if (uploadResponse.status !== 200) throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${uploadResponse.body}`);
          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) throw new Error('Failed to generate signed URL');
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);
          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
          } else {
            setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
            onError={(e) => {
              console.log('Image Load Error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
              setProfilePic(null);
            }}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, ScrollView, Platform, Keyboard } from 'react-native';
import { useRoute, useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import theme from '../constants/theme';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'employer' };
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded with role:', role);
    const fetchUserData = async () => {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (user) {
        console.log('User ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              setProfilePic(null);
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile_pics in data');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No authenticated user');
      }
    };
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Image pick triggered');
      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaType.IMAGE, // Fixed warning
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);
      if (!result.canceled && result.assets) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        if (user) {
          const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
          const fileExt = fileUri.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
          const mimeType = fileExt === 'jpg' || fileExt === 'jpeg' ? 'image/jpeg' : 'image/png';
          const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
          if (!session) throw new Error('No active session');
          console.log('Attempting to remove file:', fileName);
          await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove([fileName]);
          const uploadResponse = await FileSystem.uploadAsync(
            `${supabase.storageUrl}/object/pics/${fileName}`,
            fileUri,
            {
              headers: {
                'Content-Type': mimeType,
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${session.access_token}`,
              },
              httpMethod: 'PUT',
              uploadType: FileSystem.FileSystemUploadType.BINARY_CONTENT,
            }
          );
          console.log('Upload response:', uploadResponse);
          if (uploadResponse.status !== 200) throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${uploadResponse.body}`);
          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) throw new Error('Failed to generate signed URL');
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);
          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save pic URL: ' + updateError.message);
          } else {
            setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
          }
        }
      } else if (result.canceled) {
        console.log('Image pick cancelled');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Error picking image:', error);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (user) {
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed.');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
    if (error) {
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed.');
    } else {
      console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
      navigation.reset({
        index: 0,
        routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
      });
    }
  };

  const dismissKeyboard = () => {
    Keyboard.dismiss();
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      style={styles.container}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={localStyles.scrollContainer}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
          <Image
            source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
            style={[localStyles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60 }]}
            onError={(e) => {
              console.log('Image Load Error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
              setProfilePic(null);
            }}
          />
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
        <View style={localStyles.bioContainer}>
          <TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={businessName}
            onChangeText={setBusinessName}
            placeholder="Business Name (optional)"
            multiline
          />
          {businessName.length > 0 && (
            <TouchableOpacity style={localStyles.checkmark} onPress={dismissKeyboard}>
              <Text style={localStyles.checkmarkText}>✓</Text>
            </TouchableOpacity>
          )}
        </View>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </ScrollView>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}
