import React from 'react';
import { createBottomTabNavigator } from '@react-navigation/bottom-tabs';
import { createStackNavigator } from '@react-navigation/stack';
import HomeScreen from '../screens/HomeScreen';
import ChatScreen from '../screens/ChatScreen';
import TermsScreen from '../screens/TermsScreen';
import ShareScreen from '../screens/ShareScreen';
import Icon from 'react-native-vector-icons/MaterialCommunityIcons';
import { useRoute } from '@react-navigation/native';
import WelcomeScreen from '../screens/WelcomeScreen';
import SignupScreen from '../screens/SignupScreen';
import LoginScreen from '../screens/LoginScreen';
import SeekerProfileScreen from '../screens/SeekerProfileScreen';

const Tab = createBottomTabNavigator();
const Stack = createStackNavigator();

function ProfileScreen() {
  const route = useRoute();
  const { role } = route.params || { role: 'seeker' };
  return role === 'employer' ? null : <SeekerProfileScreen />;
}

function MainTabs() {
  return (
    <Tab.Navigator
      screenOptions={({ route }) => ({
        tabBarIcon: ({ color, size }) => {
          let iconName;
          if (route.name === 'Home') iconName = 'home';
          if (route.name === 'Chat') iconName = 'chat';
          if (route.name === 'Profile') iconName = 'account';
          if (route.name === 'Terms') iconName = 'file-document';
          if (route.name === 'Share') iconName = 'share';
          return <Icon name={iconName} size={size} color={color} />;
        },
        headerShown: false,
      })}
    >
      <Tab.Screen name="Home" component={HomeScreen} initialParams={{ role: 'seeker' }} />
      <Tab.Screen name="Chat" component={ChatScreen} />
      <Tab.Screen name="Profile" component={ProfileScreen} />
      <Tab.Screen name="Terms" component={TermsScreen} />
      <Tab.Screen name="Share" component={ShareScreen} />
    </Tab.Navigator>
  );
}

export default function AppNavigator() {
  return (
    <Stack.Navigator initialRouteName="Welcome">
      <Stack.Screen name="Welcome" component={WelcomeScreen} />
      <Stack.Screen name="Signup" component={SignupScreen} />
      <Stack.Screen name="Login" component={LoginScreen} />
      <Stack.Screen name="Main" component={MainTabs} options={{ headerShown: false }} />
    </Stack.Navigator>
  );
}

import React from 'react';

Step 1: Verify Role Passing in LoginScreen.js
The bio field showing means SeekerProfileScreen is likely rendered. The AppNavigator.js ProfileScreen logs the role, but the role might not be passed correctly from LoginScreen.js to MainTabs. Update LoginScreen.js to ensure the role is passed to the Profile screen:

javascript




import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform, Image } from 'react-native';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';
import supabase from '../supabase';

export default function LoginScreen({ navigation }) {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');

  const handleLogin = async () => {
    console.log('handleLogin called');
    if (!email || !password) {
      console.log('Fields missing:', { email, password });
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Email and Password are required.');
      return;
    }

    const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
      email,
      password,
    });

    if (error) {
      console.log('Supabase error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Login Failed', error.message.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + error.message.slice(1) + '.');
    } else {
      console.log('Login successful, fetching user role');
      const userId = data.user.id;
      const { data: userData, error: dbError } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .select('role')
        .eq('id', userId)
        .single();

      if (dbError) {
        console.log('Database error:', dbError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user role.');
      } else {
        const role = userData.role;
        console.log('User role:', role);
        navigation.replace('Main', { screen: 'Profile', params: { role } }); // Pass role to Profile
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView
      style={{ flex: 1 }}
      behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'}
      keyboardVerticalOffset={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 0 : 40}
    >
      <View style={styles.container}>
        <Image
          source={require('../assets/logo.png')}
          style={styles.logo}
          resizeMode="contain"
        />
        <Text style={styles.title}>Izzijobs</Text>
        <TextInput
          style={styles.input}
          value={email}
          onChangeText={setEmail}
          placeholder="Email"
          autoCapitalize="none"
          keyboardType="email-address"
        />
        <TextInput
          style={styles.input}
          value={password}
          onChangeText={setPassword}
          placeholder="Password"
          secureTextEntry={true}
          autoCapitalize="none"
        />
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogin}>
          <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Log In</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={() => navigation.navigate('Signup')}>
          <Text style={[styles.link, { textAlign: 'center' }]}>Don't have an account? Sign Up</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}
Step 2: Fix Upload Error
The "The resource already exists" error suggests the remove operation isn’t working, possibly due to incorrect file paths or permissions. Let’s list and clear existing files in the pics bucket to ensure a clean slate, then retry the upload.

Run this SQL in Supabase SQL Editor to list files:

sql



SELECT name FROM storage.objects WHERE bucket_id = 'pics';
Manually delete all files in the pics bucket via Supabase Dashboard > Storage > pics, or run this JavaScript to clear programmatically:

javascript




const { data, error } = await supabase.storage.from('pics').list('public');
if (error) {
  console.log('List error:', error.message);
} else {
  const files = data.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
  const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage.from('pics').remove(files);
  if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
  else console.log('Files removed:', files);
}
Add this to EmployerProfileScreen.js temporarily in the handleImagePick function before the upload, then remove after testing.

Anyway, here is the current employer profile screen:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null); // Ensure default avatar is used
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    console.log('ImagePicker module:', ImagePicker);
    try {
      if (!ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync) {
        console.log('ImagePicker module missing');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Image picker module not available.');
        return;
      }

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied for image picker');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos is required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets && result.assets.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG images are supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        const fileContent = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });

        // Validate base64 string length
        if (!fileContent || fileContent.length < 100) {
          console.log('Invalid base64 content: too short');
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Invalid image data.');
          return;
        }

        const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .upload(fileName, fileContent, {
            contentType: mimeType,
            upsert: true,
          });

        if (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
          return;
        }

        const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
        if (urlError) {
          console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
          return;
        }
        console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

        const { error: updateError } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
          .eq('id', user.id);
        if (updateError) {
          console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
          return;
        }

        // Refresh user data to ensure image loads
        await fetchUserData();
        console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
      } else {
        console.log('Image picker canceled or no assets returned');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error)}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

The profile picture issue persists due to an "unknown image format" error when loading the image, despite successful uploads to Supabase. The logs show the signed URL is generated correctly, but the image fails to display. The Grok.com interface change (missing 'Attach' function) is unrelated to the code but noted—likely a temporary UI update or bug on grok.com. Below are steps to fix the profile picture issue.

Issue Analysis
Upload Success: The image uploads to the pics bucket, and the signed URL is generated (e.g., https://nkrnkzbunmjtnqforuit.supabase.co/storage/...).
Error: Image load error: unknown image format suggests the image is corrupted, incompatible, or not processed correctly by React Native's <Image> component.
Possible Causes:
File corruption during upload (base64 encoding issue).
Supabase storage returning an invalid or unsupported image format.
React Native <Image> component failing to render the signed URL due to format or network issues.
Fix Steps
Ensure Proper File Conversion:
Modify handleImagePick to use a Blob instead of base64 to avoid encoding issues. Update the upload logic:

javascript




const handleImagePick = async () => {
  console.log('Image pick triggered');
  try {
    const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
    if (status !== 'granted') {
      console.log('Permission denied');
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
      return;
    }

    const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
      mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
      quality: 0.8,
      allowsEditing: true,
    });
    console.log('Picker result:', result);

    if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
      const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
      const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
      if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
        console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
        return;
      }

      setProfilePic(fileUri);
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
      console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

      // Fetch file as Blob
      const response = await fetch(fileUri);
      const fileBlob = await response.blob();

      const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
        .from('pics')
        .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
          contentType: mimeType,
          upsert: true,
        });

      if (uploadError) {
        console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
        return;
      }

      const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
        .from('pics')
        .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
      if (urlError) {
        console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
        return;
      }
      console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

      const { error: updateError } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (updateError) {
        console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
        return;
      }

      await fetchUserData();
      console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
      Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
    Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
  }
};
Verify Supabase Storage:

Check the pics bucket in Supabase Dashboard > Storage to confirm the uploaded file (public/profile-4bf1ee89-f4ac-4370-9469-ada8e583b54b-1753792050112.jpg) is a valid JPEG.

Download the file manually and open it to ensure it’s not corrupted.

Ensure the pics bucket has a policy allowing public read access:

sql



CREATE POLICY "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');
Handle Image Rendering:

Add cache control to the signed URL to prevent stale images:

javascript




const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
  .from('pics')
  .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60, {
    transform: { format: 'jpeg' }, // Force JPEG format
  });
Update the <Image> component to handle errors and use a fallback:

javascript




<Image
  source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
  style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
  onError={(e) => {
    console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
    setProfilePic(null); // Fallback to default if error
  }}
/>

Below is the updated EmployerProfileScreen.js with the createSignedUrl changes applied (adding transform: { format: 'jpeg' } in two places) and the other fixes from the previous response (Blob upload and image cache handling). I've integrated all changes into the full file for clarity.

javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60, {
                transform: { format: 'jpeg' }, // Force JPEG format
              });
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null); // Ensure default avatar is used
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Fetch file as Blob
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const fileBlob = await response.blob();

        const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
            contentType: mimeType,
            upsert: true,
          });

        if (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
          return;
        }

        const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60, {
            transform: { format: 'jpeg' }, // Force JPEG format
          });
        if (urlError) {
          console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
          return;
        }
        console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

        const { error: updateError } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
          .eq('id', user.id);
        if (updateError) {
          console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
          return;
        }

        await fetchUserData();
        console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null); // Fallback to default if error
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
Changes Applied
Signed URL Transform: Added transform: { format: 'jpeg' } to both createSignedUrl calls (in fetchUserData and handleImagePick) to ensure JPEG format.
Blob Upload: Replaced base64 encoding with Blob-based upload in handleImagePick to prevent corruption.
Image Cache: Added cache: 'reload' to the <Image> component to avoid stale images.
Error Handling: Kept the fallback to default avatar if the image fails to load.

The logs show two issues:

Signed URL Error: body/transform/format must be equal to one of the allowed values indicates Supabase doesn't support transform: { format: 'jpeg' } in createSignedUrl. This is likely due to an outdated Supabase client or unsupported transform options.
Upload Error: Network request failed during image upload suggests a connectivity issue or incorrect Blob handling.
Fixes
Remove Transform Option: Since transform: { format: 'jpeg' } is causing an error, remove it from both createSignedUrl calls. Supabase should serve the image as uploaded (JPEG/PNG).
Fix Blob Upload: The Network request failed error may stem from Blob handling or Supabase server issues. Ensure the Blob is correctly formatted and retry the upload with error logging.
Clear Existing Files: The profile picture remains due to a stale file in the pics bucket. Clear the bucket to avoid conflicts.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async () => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files for this user
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Fetch file as Blob
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const fileBlob = await response.blob();
        console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.size);

        const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
            contentType: mimeType,
            upsert: true,
          });

        if (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
          return;
        }

        const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
        if (urlError) {
          console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
          return;
        }
        console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

        const { error: updateError } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
          .eq('id', user.id);
        if (updateError) {
          console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
          return;
        }

        await fetchUserData();
        console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
Changes Made
Removed Transform: Deleted transform: { format: 'jpeg' } from both createSignedUrl calls to fix the body/transform/format error.
Added File Cleanup: Added logic in handleImagePick to list and remove existing user profile pictures before uploading a new one to prevent conflicts.
Enhanced Blob Logging: Added console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.size) to verify Blob creation.
Kept Cache Handling: Retained cache: 'reload' in the <Image> component.

Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                // Clear invalid profile_pics
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Fetch file as Blob
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const fileBlob = await response.blob();
        console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.size);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
Changes Made
Clear Invalid Profile Pic: Added logic in fetchUserData to reset profile_pics to null if Object not found occurs.
Retry Upload: Modified handleImagePick to retry uploads up to 2 times on network errors.
Kept File Cleanup: Retained logic to clear existing user files before upload.

sql



CREATE POLICY "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');

The Supabase storage log shows the upload error No content provided (HTTP 400), indicating the Blob sent to Supabase is empty or malformed. The client log confirms Network request failed, and the Blob size: 47732 suggests the Blob is created but not transmitted correctly. The profile_pics: null in the database is expected after the previous Object not found fix.

Issue Analysis
Root Cause: The fetch(fileUri).blob() call may produce an invalid Blob, or the Supabase client (supabase-js-react-native/2.52.1) fails to send it properly, possibly due to a bug or network issue.
Supabase Client: Version 2.52.1 is outdated (latest is ~2.55.0 as of July 2025).
Network: The Network request failed error suggests a potential connectivity issue or server rejection.
Fixes
Update Supabase Client: Update to the latest @supabase/supabase-js to fix potential Blob handling bugs:
bash




npm install @supabase/supabase-js@latest
Switch to ArrayBuffer Upload: Replace Blob with ArrayBuffer to ensure proper file transmission.
Add Network Retry Logic: Enhance retry logic with a delay to handle transient network issues.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Fetch file as ArrayBuffer
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const arrayBuffer = await response.arrayBuffer();
        console.log('ArrayBuffer size:', arrayBuffer.byteLength);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, arrayBuffer, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000); // 1-second delay
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2






Interrupted

The ERESOLVE error occurs because @geoapify/react-geocoder-autocomplete@2.0.1 requires react@^18.2.0, but your project uses react@19.0.0, causing a peer dependency conflict. Additionally, the Supabase storage error (No content provided) and Network request failed persist.

Fix Dependency Conflict
Force Install Supabase: Use --legacy-peer-deps to bypass the conflict:
bash




npm install @supabase/supabase-js@latest --legacy-peer-deps

json



"dependencies": {
  "react": "18.3.1",
  "react-native": "0.76.0",
  ...
}
Then run:
bash




npm install
Fix Supabase Upload
The No content provided error suggests the ArrayBuffer isn't sent correctly. Switch to FileSystem.readAsStringAsync with base64 encoding, which is more reliable for React Native.

Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Read file as base64
        const base64 = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });
        console.log('Base64 length:', base64.length);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, Buffer.from(base64, 'base64'), {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
Next Steps
Run npm install @supabase/supabase-js@latest --legacy-peer-deps.
Replace EmployerProfileScreen.js with the code above.
Verify pics bucket permissions in Supabase:
sql



CREATE POLICY "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');
