The 2 pics in the storage bucket 'pics' is from this morning.

If you want, we can delete this bucket, install a new one with sql, and see what happens?




The error Property 'Buffer' doesn't exist occurs because Buffer is not available in React Native (it's a Node.js feature). The Supabase log shows a bucket list operation, not an upload, and the two files in the pics bucket are stale. Deleting and recreating the bucket is a good idea to ensure a clean state. Let's fix the upload by replacing Buffer with a direct base64 string and recreate the bucket.

Fix Upload Code
Replace Buffer.from(base64, 'base64') with the base64 string directly in EmployerProfileScreen.js.

Recreate Pics Bucket
Delete Existing Bucket:
Go to Supabase Dashboard > Storage > pics > Delete all files, then delete the bucket.
Recreate Bucket with SQL: Run in Supabase SQL Editor:
sql



INSERT INTO storage.buckets (id, name, public) VALUES ('pics', 'pics', true);
Set Permissions:
sql



CREATE POLICY "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');
CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Read file as base64
        const base64 = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });
        console.log('Base64 length:', base64.length);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, base64, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
              contentEncoding: 'base64',
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

Fix Storage Policy
The current INSERT policy may not allow uploads to the public folder in the pics bucket. Update the policy to explicitly allow authenticated users to insert objects in the public folder.

Steps
Update Storage Policies: Run in Supabase SQL Editor:
sql



-- Drop existing policies to avoid conflicts
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects;

-- Create new policies
CREATE POLICY "Allow public read access" ON storage.objects
FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');

CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated' AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public');

CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated' AND (storage.foldername(name))[1] = 'public');

The error new row violates row-level security policy occurs during the upload to the pics bucket, indicating the INSERT policy is still not allowing the operation.

Issue Analysis

The Base64 length: 63644 confirms the file is properly encoded, so the issue is with the Supabase storage policy or bucket setup.
Fix Storage Policy

FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'anon');

CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated write access" ON storage.objects
FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');

CREATE POLICY "Allow authenticated delete access" ON storage.objects
FOR DELETE USING (bucket_id = 'pics' AND auth.role() = 'authenticated');

Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError || !user) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError?.message || 'No user');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'User not authenticated.');
        return;
      }
      console.log('Authenticated user ID:', user.id);

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Read file as base64
        const base64 = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });
        console.log('Base64 length:', base64.length);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, base64, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
              contentEncoding: 'base64',
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

 LOG  Profile picture uploaded successfully

The logs show the image uploads successfully (Profile picture uploaded successfully), and a signed URL is generated, but the Image load error: unknown image format causes the profile picture to revert to the default avatar. This suggests the uploaded file in the pics bucket is corrupted or not recognized as a valid image by React Native's <Image> component, despite being a JPEG.

Issue Analysis
Upload Success: The file (public/profile-4bf1ee89-f4ac-4370-9469-ada8e583b54b-1753799709921.jpg) is uploaded, and the signed URL is generated.
Error Cause: The unknown image format error likely stems from:
Base64 encoding/decoding corruption during upload.
Supabase not storing the file correctly as a JPEG.
React Native's <Image> component failing to render the signed URL.
Fix Steps
Switch to Blob Upload: Replace base64 with Blob to avoid encoding issues, as base64 may introduce corruption.
Verify File in Supabase: Manually download the uploaded file from Supabase to confirm it’s a valid JPEG.
Increase Signed URL Expiry: Extend the signed URL expiry to prevent premature expiration.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 24 * 60 * 60); // 24-hour expiry
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError || !user) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError?.message || 'No user');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'User not authenticated.');
        return;
      }
      console.log('Authenticated user ID:', user.id);

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Fetch file as Blob
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const fileBlob = await response.blob();
        console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.size);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 24 * 60 * 60); // 24-hour expiry
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

"mimeType": "image/jpeg", "rotation": null, "type": "image", "uri": "file:///data/user/0/host.exp.exponent/cache/ExperienceData/%2540anonymous%252Fizzijobs-2af31e08-7248-44d8-b132-1c529e4ee767/ImagePicker/443232d5-bdf8-4bb3-ac4b-c57fe7855c09.jpeg", "width": 1280}], "canceled": false}

The logs show two issues:

Image Load Error: The users table references public/profile-4bf1ee89-f4ac-4370-9469-ada8e583b54b-1753800076370.jpg, but Image load error: unknown image format occurs, and the pics bucket is empty, indicating the file doesn’t exist or is corrupted.
Upload Error: New uploads fail with Network request failed, suggesting a connectivity or Supabase client issue during Blob upload.
The picture still showing on your phone is likely due to a cached local URI (fileUri) from a previous upload attempt, not the actual Supabase file.

Fix Steps
Clear Stale Database Reference: Reset profile_pics to null since the referenced file doesn’t exist.
Switch Back to Base64 Upload: The Blob upload is failing (Network request failed). Revert to base64, which previously succeeded, to bypass potential Blob transmission issues.
Debug Network Issue: Log detailed network errors to diagnose Network request failed.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
              .from('pics')
              .createSignedUrl(data.profile_pics, 24 * 60 * 60);
            if (urlError) {
              console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
              if (urlError.message.includes('Object not found')) {
                await supabase
                  .from('users')
                  .update({ profile_pics: null })
                  .eq('id', user.id);
                setProfilePic(null);
              }
              Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to load profile picture.');
            } else {
              console.log('Signed URL fetched:', urlData.signedUrl);
              setProfilePic(urlData.signedUrl);
            }
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError || !user) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError?.message || 'No user');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'User not authenticated.');
        return;
      }
      console.log('Authenticated user ID:', user.id);

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Read file as base64
        const base64 = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });
        console.log('Base64 length:', base64.length);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, base64, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
              contentEncoding: 'base64',
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .createSignedUrl(fileName, 24 * 60 * 60);
          if (urlError) {
            console.log('Signed URL error:', urlError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to generate signed URL: ' + urlError.message);
            return;
          }
          console.log('Signed URL:', urlData.signedUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

The logs confirm the image uploads successfully to the pics bucket (Profile picture uploaded successfully, Base64 length: 78732), and the users table is updated with the file path. However, the Image load error: unknown image format causes the image to revert to the default avatar, indicating the uploaded file is not recognized as a valid JPEG by React Native's <Image> component, despite being stored in Supabase.

Issue Analysis
Upload Success: The file (public/profile-4bf1ee89-f4ac-4370-9469-ada8e583b54b-1753800599150.jpg) is uploaded, and a signed URL is generated.
Error Cause: The unknown image format error suggests:
The base64-encoded file is corrupted during upload or storage.
Supabase is not storing the file correctly as a JPEG.
React Native's <Image> component fails to render the signed URL due to format issues.
Previous Files: The log shows older files being cleared correctly (Cleared existing files).
Fix Steps
Verify File Integrity: Download the uploaded file from Supabase to confirm it’s a valid JPEG.
Add Content-Type Header: Ensure the signed URL includes the correct Content-Type to help React Native recognize the image format.
Use Public URL: Test using a public URL instead of a signed URL, as the pics bucket is public.
Clear Cache and Retry: Clear Expo cache to rule out caching issues.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const publicUrl = `${supabase.storage.from('pics').getPublicUrl(data.profile_pics).data.publicUrl}`;
            console.log('Public URL fetched:', publicUrl);
            setProfilePic(publicUrl);
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError || !user) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError?.message || 'No user');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'User not authenticated.');
        return;
      }
      console.log('Authenticated user ID:', user.id);

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Read file as base64
        const base64 = await FileSystem.readAsStringAsync(fileUri, {
          encoding: FileSystem.EncodingType.Base64,
        });
        console.log('Base64 length:', base64.length);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, base64, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
              contentEncoding: 'base64',
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const publicUrl = `${supabase.storage.from('pics').getPublicUrl(fileName).data.publicUrl}`;
          console.log('Public URL:', publicUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

The logs confirm the image uploads successfully (Profile picture uploaded successfully, Base64 length: 78732), and the users table updates with the file path (public/profile-4bf1ee89-f4ac-4370-9469-ada8e583b54b-1753801022109.jpg). However, the Image load error: unknown image format and your confirmation that the downloaded file is not a valid JPEG indicate the base64-encoded file is corrupted during upload or storage, causing React Native's <Image> component to fail and revert to the default avatar.

Issue Analysis
Upload Success: The file is uploaded to the pics bucket, and the public URL is generated.
Corruption Cause: The base64 data is likely corrupted due to improper handling in @supabase/supabase-js or a mismatch in contentEncoding. The unknown image format error occurs because the stored file is not a valid JPEG.
Public URL: Using public URLs works, but the file itself is invalid.
Fix Steps
Switch to Blob Upload with Explicit MIME Type: Revert to Blob upload to avoid base64 encoding issues, ensuring the correct MIME type is set.
Clear Stale Database Reference: Reset profile_pics to prevent referencing invalid files.
Verify File Upload: Check the uploaded file’s integrity in Supabase.
Updated EmployerProfileScreen.js
javascript




import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';
import supabase from '../supabase';
import { styles } from '../constants/styles';

export default function EmployerProfileScreen() {
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');
  const [businessName, setBusinessName] = useState('');
  const [profilePic, setProfilePic] = useState(null);

  const fetchUserData = async () => {
    console.log('Starting fetchUserData');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to authenticate user.');
        return;
      }
      if (user) {
        console.log('Fetching data for user ID:', user.id);
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .select('name, email, phone, business_name, profile_pics')
          .eq('id', user.id)
          .single();
        if (error) {
          console.log('Fetch error:', error.message);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Could not fetch user data: ' + error.message);
        } else {
          console.log('Fetched employer data:', data);
          setName(data.name || '');
          setEmail(data.email || '');
          setPhone(data.phone || '');
          setBusinessName(data.business_name || '');
          if (data.profile_pics) {
            const publicUrl = `${supabase.storage.from('pics').getPublicUrl(data.profile_pics).data.publicUrl}`;
            console.log('Public URL fetched:', publicUrl);
            setProfilePic(publicUrl);
          } else {
            console.log('No profile picture found, using default');
            setProfilePic(null);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log('No user found');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('fetchUserData error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to fetch user data: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    console.log('EmployerProfileScreen loaded');
    fetchUserData();
  }, []);

  const delay = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  const handleImagePick = async (retryCount = 0) => {
    console.log('Image pick triggered');
    try {
      const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (authError || !user) {
        console.log('Auth error:', authError?.message || 'No user');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'User not authenticated.');
        return;
      }
      console.log('Authenticated user ID:', user.id);

      const { status } = await ImagePicker.requestMediaLibraryPermissionsAsync();
      if (status !== 'granted') {
        console.log('Permission denied');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Permission to access photos required.');
        return;
      }

      const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
        mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
        quality: 0.8,
        allowsEditing: true,
      });
      console.log('Picker result:', result);

      if (!result.canceled && result.assets?.length > 0) {
        const fileUri = result.assets[0].uri;
        const mimeType = result.assets[0].mimeType;
        if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png'].includes(mimeType)) {
          console.log('Invalid file format:', mimeType);
          Alert.alert('Error', 'Only JPEG or PNG supported.');
          return;
        }

        setProfilePic(fileUri);
        const fileName = `public/profile-${user.id}-${Date.now()}.jpg`;
        console.log('Preparing to upload file:', fileName);

        // Clear existing files
        const { data: existingFiles, error: listError } = await supabase.storage
          .from('pics')
          .list('public', { search: `profile-${user.id}` });
        if (listError) {
          console.log('List error:', listError.message);
        } else if (existingFiles.length > 0) {
          const filesToDelete = existingFiles.map(file => `public/${file.name}`);
          const { error: removeError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .remove(filesToDelete);
          if (removeError) console.log('Remove error:', removeError.message);
          else console.log('Cleared existing files:', filesToDelete);
        }

        // Fetch file as Blob
        const response = await fetch(fileUri);
        const fileBlob = await response.blob();
        console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.size);

        try {
          const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
            .from('pics')
            .upload(fileName, fileBlob, {
              contentType: mimeType,
              upsert: true,
            });

          if (uploadError) {
            console.log('Upload error:', uploadError.message);
            if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
              console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
              await delay(1000);
              return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
            }
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to upload image: ' + uploadError.message);
            return;
          }

          const publicUrl = `${supabase.storage.from('pics').getPublicUrl(fileName).data.publicUrl}`;
          console.log('Public URL:', publicUrl);

          const { error: updateError } = await supabase
            .from('users')
            .update({ profile_pics: fileName })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (updateError) {
            console.log('Database update error:', updateError.message);
            Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile picture path: ' + updateError.message);
            return;
          }

          await fetchUserData();
          console.log('Profile picture uploaded successfully');
          Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile picture uploaded!');
        } catch (uploadError) {
          console.log('Upload attempt error:', uploadError.message);
          if (uploadError.message.includes('Network') && retryCount < 2) {
            console.log(`Retrying upload attempt ${retryCount + 1}`);
            await delay(1000);
            return handleImagePick(retryCount + 1);
          }
          throw uploadError;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Image pick error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to process image: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    console.log('Saving employer profile');
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
      if (!user) {
        console.log('No user found for save');
        Alert.alert('Error', 'No authenticated user found.');
        return;
      }
      const { error } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .update({ name, email, phone, business_name: businessName })
        .eq('id', user.id);
      if (error) {
        console.log('Save error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Save failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Employer profile saved');
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Profile saved!');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Save error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to save profile: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    console.log('Logout triggered');
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
      if (error) {
        console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Logout failed: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        console.log('Navigating to Welcome screen');
        navigation.reset({
          index: 0,
          routes: [{ name: 'Welcome' }],
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Logout error:', error.message);
      Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to logout: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <TouchableOpacity onPress={handleImagePick}>
        <Image
          source={profilePic ? { uri: profilePic, cache: 'reload' } : require('../assets/default-avatar.png')}
          style={[styles.profilePic, { width: 120, height: 120, borderRadius: 60, alignSelf: 'center', margin: 20 }]}
          onError={(e) => {
            console.log('Image load error:', e.nativeEvent.error);
            setProfilePic(null);
          }}
        />
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={name} onChangeText={setName} placeholder="Name" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} placeholder="Email" keyboardType="email-address" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={phone} onChangeText={setPhone} placeholder="Phone" keyboardType="phone-pad" />
      <TextInput style={styles.input} value={businessName} onChangeText={setBusinessName} placeholder="Business Name (optional)" />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleSave}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Save</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.button} onPress={handleLogout}>
        <Text style={{ color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

A subsequent Blob upload attempt fails with Network request failed. The pics bucket stores the file, but it’s corrupted, causing React Native’s <Image> component to revert to the default avatar.

Issue Analysis
Base64 Upload: Succeeds but produces a corrupted file (unknown image format).
Blob Upload: Fails with Network request failed, likely due to connectivity or Supabase client issues.
Corruption Cause: The base64 encoding/decoding process may be mishandled by @supabase/supabase-js, or the file is not stored correctly as a JPEG.
Fix Steps
Clear Stale Database Reference: Reset profile_pics to avoid referencing corrupted files.
Use File Object Upload: Switch to uploading the file directly as a File object to avoid base64 and Blob issues.
Debug Network Error: Log detailed network errors for Blob upload failure.

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Image, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, Alert, ScrollView } from 'react-native';
import { useNavigation } from '@react-navigation/native';
import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker';

  const navigation = useNavigation();
